<s> his pulse is good <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>

<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>
<s> there's only me here <\s>
<s> they don't waste their time hurrying down in the morning <\s>
<s> why it must be two years since we had the pleasure of seeing you <\s>
<s> nervously what have you been doing with yourself <\s>
<s> impressed if you want to see him he points to cokeson's chair he'll be here directly never misses not much <\s>
<s> delicately i hope our friend's back from the country <\s>
<s> his time's been up these three months if i remember <\s>
<s> ruth nods i was awful sorry about that <\s>
<s> the governor made a mistake if you ask me <\s>
<s> he ought to have given him a chanst <\s>
<s> and i say the judge ought to ha let him go after that <\s>
<s> they've forgot what human nature's like <\s>
<s> ruth gives him a honeyed smile sweedle <\s>
<s> they come down on you like a cartload of bricks flatten you out and when you don't swell up again they complain of it <\s>
<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>
<s> he shakes his head in the plenitude of wisdom why only the other day the governor but cokeson has come in through the outer office brisk with east wind and decidedly greyer <\s>
<s> drawing off his coat and gloves why <\s>
<s> then motioning sweedle out and closing the door quite a stranger <\s>
<s> must be two years <\s>
<s> d'you want to see me <\s>
<s> i can give you a minute <\s>
<s> i'm not living where i was <\s>
<s> eyeing her askance i hope things are more comfortable at home <\s>
<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>
<s> beginning to feel that things are not so jolly as ha had hoped well i'm glad to have seen you <\s>
<s> you've not heard from the young man i suppose since he came out <\s>
<s> yes i ran across him yesterday <\s>
<s> i hope he's well <\s>
<s> with sudden fierceness he can't get anything to do <\s>
<s> it's dreadful to see him <\s>
<s> he's just skin and bone <\s>
<s> with genuine concern dear me <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to hear that <\s>
<s> on his guard again didn't they find him a place when his time was up <\s>
<s> he was only there three weeks <\s>
<s> i'm sure i don't know what i can do for you <\s>
<s> i don't like to be snubby <\s>
<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>
<s> scanning her not unprosperous figure i know his relations aren't very forthy about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>
<s> staring at her disturbed i'm a family man i don't want to hear anything unpleasant <\s>
<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>
<s> nothing wrong with his eyes <\s>
<s> his pulse is good <\s>
<s> it doesn't amount to melancholia <\s>
<s> shaking his head i can report on him if you like but if i do i ought to report on others <\s>
<s> looking towards falder's cell the poor devil must just stick it then <\s>
<s> as he says thin he looks absently at wooder <\s>
<s> for answer the governor stares at him turns on his heel and walks away <\s>
<s> there is a sound as of beating on metal <\s>
<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>
<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>

<s> as he says thin he looks absently at wooder <\s>
<s> for answer the governor stares at him turns on his heel and walks away <\s>
<s> there is a sound as of beating on metal <\s>
<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>
<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>

<s> there is a sound as of beating on metal <\s>
<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>
<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>
<s> there's only me here <\s>

<s> why it must be two years since we had the pleasure of seeing you <\s>
<s> nervously what have you been doing with yourself <\s>

<s> ruth nods i was awful sorry about that <\s>
<s> the governor made a mistake if you ask me <\s>
<s> he ought to have given him a chanst <\s>
<s> and i say the judge ought to ha let him go after that <\s>
<s> they've forgot what human nature's like <\s>
<s> ruth gives him a honeyed smile sweedle <\s>
<s> they come down on you like a cartload of bricks flatten you out and when you don't swell up again they complain of it <\s>
<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>

<s> drawing off his coat and gloves why <\s>
<s> then motioning sweedle out and closing the door quite a stranger <\s>

<s> i can give you a minute <\s>

<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>
<s> beginning to feel that things are not so jolly as ha had hoped well i'm glad to have seen you <\s>
<s> you've not heard from the young man i suppose since he came out <\s>

<s> i hope he's well <\s>

<s> i'm sorry to hear that <\s>

<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>
<s> scanning her not unprosperous figure i know his relations aren't very forthy about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>

<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>

<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>
<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>
<s> there's only me here <\s>
<s> they don't waste their time hurrying down in the morning <\s>
<s> why it must be two years since we had the pleasure of seeing you <\s>
<s> nervously what have you been doing with yourself <\s>

<s> delicately i hope our friend's back from the country <\s>
<s> his time's been up these three months if i remember <\s>
<s> ruth nods i was awful sorry about that <\s>
<s> the governor made a mistake if you ask me <\s>
<s> he ought to have given him a chanst <\s>
<s> and i say the judge ought to ha let him go after that <\s>
<s> they've forgot what human nature's like <\s>
<s> ruth gives him a honeyed smile sweedle <\s>
<s> they come down on you like a cartload of bricks flatten you out and when you don't swell up again they complain of it <\s>
<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>
<s> he shakes his head in the plenitude of wisdom why only the other day the governor but cokeson has come in through the outer office brisk with east wind and decidedly greyer <\s>
<s> drawing off his coat and gloves why <\s>
<s> then motioning sweedle out and closing the door quite a stranger <\s>
<s> must be two years <\s>
<s> d'you want to see me <\s>
<s> i can give you a minute <\s>
<s> i'm not living where i was <\s>
<s> eyeing her askance i hope things are more comfortable at home <\s>
<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>
<s> beginning to feel that things are not so jolly as ha had hoped well i'm glad to have seen you <\s>
<s> you've not heard from the young man i suppose since he came out <\s>
<s> yes i ran across him yesterday <\s>
<s> i hope he's well <\s>
<s> with sudden fierceness he can't get anything to do <\s>
<s> it's dreadful to see him <\s>
<s> he's just skin and bone <\s>
<s> with genuine concern dear me <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to hear that <\s>
<s> on his guard again didn't they find him a place when his time was up <\s>
<s> he was only there three weeks <\s>
<s> i'm sure i don't know what i can do for you <\s>
<s> i don't like to be snubby <\s>
<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>
<s> scanning her not unprosperous figure i know his relations aren't very forthy about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>
<s> staring at her disturbed i'm a family man i don't want to hear anything unpleasant <\s>
<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>
<s> nothing wrong with his eyes <\s>
<s> his pulse is good <\s>
<s> it doesn't amount to melancholia <\s>
<s> shaking his head i can report on him if you like but if i do i ought to report on others <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>

<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>
<s> there's only me here <\s>
<s> they don't waste their time hurrying down in the morning <\s>
<s> why it must be two years since we had the pleasure of seeing you <\s>
<s> nervously what have you been doing with yourself <\s>
<s> impressed if you want to see him he points to cokeson's chair he'll be here directly never misses not much <\s>
<s> delicately i hope our friend's back from the country <\s>
<s> his time's been up these three months if i remember <\s>
<s> ruth nods i was awful sorry about that <\s>
<s> the governor made a mistake if you ask me <\s>
<s> he ought to have given him a chanst <\s>
<s> and i say the judge ought to ha let him go after that <\s>
<s> they've forgot what human nature's like <\s>
<s> ruth gives him a honeyed smile sweedle <\s>
<s> they come down on you like a cartload of bricks flatten you out and when you don't swell up again they complain of it <\s>
<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>
<s> he shakes his head in the plenitude of wisdom why only the other day the governor but cokeson has come in through the outer office brisk with east wind and decidedly greyer <\s>
<s> drawing off his coat and gloves why <\s>
<s> then motioning sweedle out and closing the door quite a stranger <\s>
<s> must be two years <\s>
<s> d'you want to see me <\s>
<s> i can give you a minute <\s>
<s> i'm not living where i was <\s>
<s> eyeing her askance i hope things are more comfortable at home <\s>
<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>
<s> beginning to feel that things are not so jolly as ha had hoped well i'm glad to have seen you <\s>
<s> you've not heard from the young man i suppose since he came out <\s>
<s> yes i ran across him yesterday <\s>
<s> i hope he's well <\s>
<s> with sudden fierceness he can't get anything to do <\s>
<s> it's dreadful to see him <\s>
<s> he's just skin and bone <\s>
<s> with genuine concern dear me <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to hear that <\s>
<s> on his guard again didn't they find him a place when his time was up <\s>
<s> he was only there three weeks <\s>
<s> i'm sure i don't know what i can do for you <\s>
<s> i don't like to be snubby <\s>
<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>
<s> scanning her not unprosperous figure i know his relations aren't very forthy about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>
<s> staring at her disturbed i'm a family man i don't want to hear anything unpleasant <\s>
<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>
<s> nothing wrong with his eyes <\s>
<s> his pulse is good <\s>
<s> it doesn't amount to melancholia <\s>
<s> shaking his head i can report on him if you like but if i do i ought to report on others <\s>
<s> looking towards falder's cell the poor devil must just stick it then <\s>
<s> as he says thin he looks absently at wooder <\s>
<s> for answer the governor stares at him turns on his heel and walks away <\s>
<s> there is a sound as of beating on metal <\s>
<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>

<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>
<s> there's only me here <\s>
<s> they don't waste their time hurrying down in the morning <\s>
<s> why it must be two years since we had the pleasure of seeing you <\s>
<s> nervously what have you been doing with yourself <\s>
<s> impressed if you want to see him he points to cokeson's chair he'll be here directly never misses not much <\s>
<s> delicately i hope our friend's back from the country <\s>
<s> his time's been up these three months if i remember <\s>
<s> ruth nods i was awful sorry about that <\s>
<s> the governor made a mistake if you ask me <\s>
<s> he ought to have given him a chanst <\s>
<s> and i say the judge ought to ha let him go after that <\s>
<s> they've forgot what human nature's like <\s>
<s> ruth gives him a honeyed smile sweedle <\s>
<s> they come down on you like a cartload of bricks flatten you out and when you don't swell up again they complain of it <\s>
<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>
<s> he shakes his head in the plenitude of wisdom why only the other day the governor but cokeson has come in through the outer office brisk with east wind and decidedly greyer <\s>
<s> drawing off his coat and gloves why <\s>
<s> then motioning sweedle out and closing the door quite a stranger <\s>
<s> must be two years <\s>
<s> d'you want to see me <\s>
<s> i can give you a minute <\s>
<s> i'm not living where i was <\s>
<s> eyeing her askance i hope things are more comfortable at home <\s>
<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>
<s> beginning to feel that things are not so jolly as ha had hoped well i'm glad to have seen you <\s>
<s> you've not heard from the young man i suppose since he came out <\s>
<s> yes i ran across him yesterday <\s>
<s> i hope he's well <\s>
<s> with sudden fierceness he can't get anything to do <\s>
<s> it's dreadful to see him <\s>
<s> he's just skin and bone <\s>
<s> with genuine concern dear me <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to hear that <\s>
<s> on his guard again didn't they find him a place when his time was up <\s>
<s> he was only there three weeks <\s>
<s> i'm sure i don't know what i can do for you <\s>
<s> i don't like to be snubby <\s>
<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>
<s> scanning her not unprosperous figure i know his relations aren't very forthy about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>
<s> staring at her disturbed i'm a family man i don't want to hear anything unpleasant <\s>
<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>
<s> nothing wrong with his eyes <\s>
<s> his pulse is good <\s>
<s> it doesn't amount to melancholia <\s>
<s> shaking his head i can report on him if you like but if i do i ought to report on others <\s>
<s> looking towards falder's cell the poor devil must just stick it then <\s>
<s> as he says thin he looks absently at wooder <\s>
<s> for answer the governor stares at him turns on his heel and walks away <\s>
<s> there is a sound as of beating on metal <\s>
<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>

<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>
<s> there's only me here <\s>

<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>

<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>
<s> beginning to feel that things are not so jolly as ha had hoped well i'm glad to have seen you <\s>

<s> i'm sorry to hear that <\s>

<s> i don't like to be snubby <\s>
<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>
<s> scanning her not unprosperous figure i know his relations aren't very forthy about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>

<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>
<s> nothing wrong with his eyes <\s>
<s> his pulse is good <\s>
<s> it doesn't amount to melancholia <\s>

<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>

<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>
<s> sweedle now blessed with a sprouting moustache is getting the offices ready <\s>
<s> he arranges papers on cokeson's table then goes to a covered washstand raises the lid and looks at himself in the mirror <\s>
<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
<s> there seems a kind of exultation and excitement behind her habitual impassivity <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing her and dropping the lid of the washstand with a bang hello <\s>

<s> i know em seen a lot of that sort of thing in my time <\s>

<s> i couldn't stay with honeywill after all <\s>
<s> you haven't done anything rash i hope <\s>
<s> i should be sorry if you'd done anything rash <\s>
<s> i've kept the children with me <\s>

<s> i can't bear his being like that <\s>

<s> perhaps you can do something for him till he finds his feet <\s>
<s> i could have but not now <\s>
<s> proudly i've seen him again that's all over <\s>

<s> excuse me i'm very busy <\s>
<s> nothing wrong with his eyes <\s>
<s> his pulse is good <\s>
<s> it doesn't amount to melancholia <\s>

<s> banging on his door sir <\s>
<s> i thought we should have more of that <\s>
<s> he hurries forward passing the governor who follows closely <\s>

<s> scene iii falder's cell a whitewashed space thirteen feet broad by seven deep and nine feet high with a rounded ceiling <\s>
<s> the floor is of shiny blackened bricks <\s>
<s> the barred window of opaque glass with a ventilator is high up in the middle of the end wall <\s>
<s> in the middle of the opposite end wall is the narrow door <\s>
<s> in a corner are the mattress and bedding rolled up two blankets two sheets and a coverlet <\s>
<s> above them is a quarter circular wooden shelf on which is a bible and several little devotional books piled in a symmetrical pyramid there are also a black hair brush tooth brush and a bit of soap <\s>
<s> in another corner is the wooden frame of a bed standing on end <\s>
<s> there is a dark ventilator under the window and another over the door <\s>
<s> falder's work a shirt to which he is putting buttonholes is hung to a nail on the wall over a small wooden table on which the novel lorna doone lies open <\s>
<s> low down in the corner by the door is a thick glass screen about a foot square covering the gas jet let into the wall <\s>
<s> there is also a wooden stool and a pair of shoes beneath it <\s>
<s> three bright round tins are set under the window <\s>
<s> in fast failing daylight falder in his stockings is seen standing motionless with his head inclined towards the door listening <\s>
<s> he moves a little closer to the door his stockinged feet making no noise <\s>
<s> he stops at the door <\s>
<s> he is trying harder and harder to hear something any little thing that is going on outside <\s>
<s> he springs suddenly upright as if at a sound and remains perfectly motionless <\s>
<s> then with a heavy sigh he moves to his work and stands looking at it with his head doom he does a stitch or two having the air of a man so lost in sadness that each stitch is as it were a coming to life <\s>
<s> then turning abruptly he begins pacing the cell moving his head like an animal pacing its cage <\s>
<s> he stops again at the door listens and placing the palms of hip hands against it with his fingers spread out leans his forehead against the iron <\s>
<s> turning from it presently he moves slowly back towards the window tracing his way with his finger along the top line of the distemper that runs round the wall <\s>
<s> he stops under the window and picking up the lid of one of the tins peers into it <\s>
<s> it has grown very nearly dark <\s>
<s> suddenly the lid falls out of his hand with a clatter the only sound that has broken the silence and he stands staring intently at the wall where the stuff of the shirt is hanging rather white in the darkness he seems to be seeing somebody or something there <\s>
<s> there is a sharp tap and click the cell light behind the glass screen has been turned up <\s>
<s> the cell is brightly lighted <\s>
<s> falder is seen gasping for breath <\s>
<s> a sound from far away as of distant dull beating on thick metal is suddenly audible <\s>
<s> falder shrinks back not able to bear this sudden clamour <\s>
<s> but the sound grows as though some great tumbril were rolling towards the cell <\s>
<s> and gradually it seems to hypnotise him <\s>
<s> he begins creeping inch by inch nearer to the door <\s>
<s> the banging sound travelling from cell to cell draws closer and closer falder's hands are seen moving as if his spirit had already joined in this beating and the sound swells till it seems to have entered the very cell <\s>
<s> he suddenly raises his clenched fists <\s>
<s> panting violently he flings himself at his door and beats on it <\s>
<s> act iv the scene is again cokeson's room at a few minutes to ten of a march morning two years later <\s>
<s> the doors are all open <\s>

<s> while he is gazing his full ruth honeywill comes in through the outer office and stands in the doorway <\s>
